# Atlas Editorial Register

This register accounts for every Markdown source file scanned from `private-source`. It is an editorial control surface, not a public SEO page.

## Summary Counts

- Total Markdown files scanned: 753
- Files published as reviewed/index (A): 18
- Files published as noindex/needs verification (B): 15
- Files published as noindex/research note (C): 0
- Files merged or marked for merge/consolidation (D): 672
- Files kept private source (E): 35
- Files marked archive/delete candidate (F): 13
- Files excluded from public build by source-folder exclusion: 753

## Type Counts

- KPI/formula: 21
- SAP diagnostic: 37
- SEO planning: 4
- agentic workflow: 634
- article idea: 8
- automation pattern: 1
- cross-domain map: 5
- giant index: 10
- process map: 25
- publishing strategy: 4
- verification backlog: 4
